+- The cited lines are real in the `260413` / `staffordersmobile.jsx` snapshot.
+- `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, and `2337` all use `*.length` inside guest-facing `pluralRu(...)` text.
+- `2333` is slightly different from the others: it counts subgroup guests with `section.orders.length`, not a top-level section total.
+- The later branch also mixes i18n styles: `2331/2333/2335/2337` use hardcoded Russian guest nouns instead of `HALL_UI_TEXT.guests`.
+
+Risks:
+
+- The prompt must define what a "guest" means: unique `order.guest`, unique guest within a session/table, or one guest per order when `guest` is missing.
+- Without that rule, an implementor can change the math differently across branches and create inconsistent totals.
+
+### Fix 2 - `activeOrders` / `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The structure exists exactly where claimed:
+- `activeOrders` filter at `3522-3545`, with the finish-stage branch at `3539-3544`
+- `filteredGroups` at `3789-3801`
+- `tabCounts` at `3804-3818`
+- The surrounding model is the real problem: `orderGroups` at `3697-3746` only stores `{ type, id, displayName, orders }`. It does **not** carry `table_session` or session open/closed state.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` both classify activity via `getStatusConfig(o).isFinishStage` plus active service requests, so any "keep served table visible until manual close" change must update both or the tabs will diverge.
+
+`closeSession` check:
+
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` exports `closeSession(sessionId)`.
+- It is used in `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx:4098`.
+- It is also used in `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981` and related copies.
+
+Risks:
+
+- A prompt that tells the implementor to change `closeSession()` is changing shared cross-page behavior, not a local SOM bug.
+- A prompt that does not explain how to detect "table still open" will force the implementor to invent new data loading or a heuristic.
+
+### Fix 3 - Ownership Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+- `2249-2252` and `2259-2262` are passive badge `<div>` nodes inside the clickable card wrapper at `2244`.
+- Those two badges do not stop propagation today.
+- The sibling "other table" lock badge at `2255-2257` already uses `e.stopPropagation()`, so the intended fix is consistent with nearby code.
+
+Risk:
+
+- The prompt should keep the fix narrowly scoped to the two passive star badges. Anything broader risks touching already-correct click handling.
+
+### Fix 4 - Remove `inProgressExpanded` Wrapper
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The four cited regions are real wrapper sites:
+- `677-703`
+- `761-769`
+- `1288-1314`
+- `1374-1398`
+- But the prompt misses another live wrapper at `2346`.
+- Shared state and effects still assume the wrapper exists:
+- `1780` initializes `inProgressExpanded`
+- `1816-1823` resets and auto-opens `expandedSubGroups` based on `inProgressExpanded`
+
+Risks:
+
+- Editing only the four listed branches leaves the `2346` branch inconsistent.
+- Removing the wrapper without revisiting `inProgressExpanded` state/effect logic leaves dead state or unintended subgroup reset behavior.
+- The prompt should enumerate all affected render branches explicitly instead of relying on line numbers alone.
+
+### Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Short reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Needs clarification | Real `.length` guest counters, but guest identity/fallback rules are unspecified |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Real structures, but session-open logic is missing and `closeSession` is shared |
+| 3 | Clear | Exact passive badge targets exist and match nearby event-handling pattern |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Four wrappers exist, but a fifth branch at `2346` is omitted and shared state still depends on the wrapper |

 ## Bottom Line
 
 For the actual file `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, this draft prompt is not execution-safe. The prompt must be rewritten against the correct snapshot before implementation starts. If the intended target is the newer `staffordersmobile.jsx` / `260413-00` architecture, the prompt should say that explicitly; if the target must remain `260306-05`, then Fixes 1, 3, and 4 need full re-scoping, and Fix 2 needs a shared-helper-safe rewrite.

+## Prompt Verification: 260414 Draft for `StaffOrdersMobile`
+
+### Scope Verified
+
+- Requested path `C:/Dev/worktrees/task-260414-045840/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` does **not** exist.
+- In that worktree, the live file is `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` in the worktree is byte-identical to local `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`.
+- Actual line count is **4193**, not `4524`.
+
+### Fix 1 - Guest Counting via `.length` + `pluralRu`
+
+Rating: **Needs clarification**
+
+- The cited lines are real in the `260413` / `staffordersmobile.jsx` snapshot.
+- `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, and `2337` all use `*.length` inside guest-facing `pluralRu(...)` text.
+- `2333` is slightly different from the others: it counts subgroup guests with `section.orders.length`, not a top-level section total.
+- The later branch also mixes i18n styles: `2331/2333/2335/2337` use hardcoded Russian guest nouns instead of `HALL_UI_TEXT.guests`.
+
+Risks:
+
+- The prompt must define what a "guest" means: unique `order.guest`, unique guest within a session/table, or one guest per order when `guest` is missing.
+- Without that rule, an implementor can change the math differently across branches and create inconsistent totals.
+
+### Fix 2 - `activeOrders` / `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The structure exists exactly where claimed:
+- `activeOrders` filter at `3522-3545`, with the finish-stage branch at `3539-3544`
+- `filteredGroups` at `3789-3801`
+- `tabCounts` at `3804-3818`
+- The surrounding model is the real problem: `orderGroups` at `3697-3746` only stores `{ type, id, displayName, orders }`. It does **not** carry `table_session` or session open/closed state.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` both classify activity via `getStatusConfig(o).isFinishStage` plus active service requests, so any "keep served table visible until manual close" change must update both or the tabs will diverge.
+
+`closeSession` check:
+
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` exports `closeSession(sessionId)`.
+- It is used in `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx:4098`.
+- It is also used in `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981` and related copies.
+
+Risks:
+
+- A prompt that tells the implementor to change `closeSession()` is changing shared cross-page behavior, not a local SOM bug.
+- A prompt that does not explain how to detect "table still open" will force the implementor to invent new data loading or a heuristic.
+
+### Fix 3 - Ownership Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+- `2249-2252` and `2259-2262` are passive badge `<div>` nodes inside the clickable card wrapper at `2244`.
+- Those two badges do not stop propagation today.
+- The sibling "other table" lock badge at `2255-2257` already uses `e.stopPropagation()`, so the intended fix is consistent with nearby code.
+
+Risk:
+
+- The prompt should keep the fix narrowly scoped to the two passive star badges. Anything broader risks touching already-correct click handling.
+
+### Fix 4 - Remove `inProgressExpanded` Wrapper
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The four cited regions are real wrapper sites:
+- `677-703`
+- `761-769`
+- `1288-1314`
+- `1374-1398`
+- But the prompt misses another live wrapper at `2346`.
+- Shared state and effects still assume the wrapper exists:
+- `1780` initializes `inProgressExpanded`
+- `1816-1823` resets and auto-opens `expandedSubGroups` based on `inProgressExpanded`
+
+Risks:
+
+- Editing only the four listed branches leaves the `2346` branch inconsistent.
+- Removing the wrapper without revisiting `inProgressExpanded` state/effect logic leaves dead state or unintended subgroup reset behavior.
+- The prompt should enumerate all affected render branches explicitly instead of relying on line numbers alone.
+
+### Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Short reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Needs clarification | Real `.length` guest counters, but guest identity/fallback rules are unspecified |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Real structures, but session-open logic is missing and `closeSession` is shared |
+| 3 | Clear | Exact passive badge targets exist and match nearby event-handling pattern |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Four wrappers exist, but a fifth branch at `2346` is omitted and shared state still depends on the wrapper |

+
+- The prompt must define what a "guest" means: unique `order.guest`, unique guest within a session/table, or one guest per order when `guest` is missing.
+- Without that rule, an implementor can change the math differently across branches and create inconsistent totals.
+
+### Fix 2 - `activeOrders` / `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The structure exists exactly where claimed:
+- `activeOrders` filter at `3522-3545`, with the finish-stage branch at `3539-3544`
+- `filteredGroups` at `3789-3801`
+- `tabCounts` at `3804-3818`
+- The surrounding model is the real problem: `orderGroups` at `3697-3746` only stores `{ type, id, displayName, orders }`. It does **not** carry `table_session` or session open/closed state.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` both classify activity via `getStatusConfig(o).isFinishStage` plus active service requests, so any "keep served table visible until manual close" change must update both or the tabs will diverge.
+
+`closeSession` check:
+
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` exports `closeSession(sessionId)`.
+- It is used in `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx:4098`.
+- It is also used in `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981` and related copies.
+
+Risks:
+
+- A prompt that tells the implementor to change `closeSession()` is changing shared cross-page behavior, not a local SOM bug.
+- A prompt that does not explain how to detect "table still open" will force the implementor to invent new data loading or a heuristic.
+
+### Fix 3 - Ownership Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+- `2249-2252` and `2259-2262` are passive badge `<div>` nodes inside the clickable card wrapper at `2244`.
+- Those two badges do not stop propagation today.

+
+Risk:
+
+- The prompt should keep the fix narrowly scoped to the two passive star badges. Anything broader risks touching already-correct click handling.
+

+- The four cited regions are real wrapper sites:
+- `677-703`

+

+- The prompt should enumerate all affected render branches explicitly instead of relying on line numbers alone.

+## Prompt Verification: 260414 Draft for `StaffOrdersMobile`

+### Scope Verified
+
+- Requested path `C:/Dev/worktrees/task-260414-045840/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` does **not** exist.

+### Fix 1 - Guest Counting via `.length` + `pluralRu`
+
+Rating: **Needs clarification**
+
+- The cited lines are real in the `260413` / `staffordersmobile.jsx` snapshot.
+- `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, and `2337` all use `*.length` inside guest-facing `pluralRu(...)` text.
+- `2333` is slightly different from the others: it counts subgroup guests with `section.orders.length`, not a top-level section total.
+- The later branch also mixes i18n styles: `2331/2333/2335/2337` use hardcoded Russian guest nouns instead of `HALL_UI_TEXT.guests`.
+
+Risks:
+
+- The prompt must define what a "guest" means: unique `order.guest`, unique guest within a session/table, or one guest per order when `guest` is missing.
+- Without that rule, an implementor can change the math differently across branches and create inconsistent totals.
+
+### Fix 2 - `activeOrders` / `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The structure exists exactly where claimed:
+- `activeOrders` filter at `3522-3545`, with the finish-stage branch at `3539-3544`
+- `filteredGroups` at `3789-3801`
+- `tabCounts` at `3804-3818`
+- The surrounding model is the real problem: `orderGroups` at `3697-3746` only stores `{ type, id, displayName, orders }`. It does **not** carry `table_session` or session open/closed state.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` both classify activity via `getStatusConfig(o).isFinishStage` plus active service requests, so any "keep served table visible until manual close" change must update both or the tabs will diverge.
+
+`closeSession` check:
+
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` exports `closeSession(sessionId)`.
+- It is used in `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx:4098`.
+- It is also used in `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981` and related copies.
+
+Risks:
+
+- A prompt that tells the implementor to change `closeSession()` is changing shared cross-page behavior, not a local SOM bug.
+- A prompt that does not explain how to detect "table still open" will force the implementor to invent new data loading or a heuristic.
+
+### Fix 3 - Ownership Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+- `2249-2252` and `2259-2262` are passive badge `<div>` nodes inside the clickable card wrapper at `2244`.
+- Those two badges do not stop propagation today.
+- The sibling "other table" lock badge at `2255-2257` already uses `e.stopPropagation()`, so the intended fix is consistent with nearby code.
+
+Risk:
+
+- The prompt should keep the fix narrowly scoped to the two passive star badges. Anything broader risks touching already-correct click handling.
+
+### Fix 4 - Remove `inProgressExpanded` Wrapper
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+- The four cited regions are real wrapper sites:
+- `677-703`
+- `761-769`
+- `1288-1314`
+- `1374-1398`
+- But the prompt misses another live wrapper at `2346`.
+- Shared state and effects still assume the wrapper exists:
+- `1780` initializes `inProgressExpanded`
+- `1816-1823` resets and auto-opens `expandedSubGroups` based on `inProgressExpanded`
+
+Risks:
+
+- Editing only the four listed branches leaves the `2346` branch inconsistent.
+- Removing the wrapper without revisiting `inProgressExpanded` state/effect logic leaves dead state or unintended subgroup reset behavior.
+- The prompt should enumerate all affected render branches explicitly instead of relying on line numbers alone.
+

+
+| Fix | Rating | Short reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Needs clarification | Real `.length` guest counters, but guest identity/fallback rules are unspecified |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Real structures, but session-open logic is missing and `closeSession` is shared |
+| 3 | Clear | Exact passive badge targets exist and match nearby event-handling pattern |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Four wrappers exist, but a fifth branch at `2346` is omitted and shared state still depends on the wrapper |

codex
The draft prompt is not execution-safe as written. The named worktree file `C:/Dev/worktrees/task-260414-045840/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` does not exist. In that worktree, the real file is `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, and it is byte-identical to local `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260413-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Actual length is `4193` lines, not `4524`.

- `Fix 1: Needs clarification.` All cited offsets are real, and `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337` all use `*.length` in guest-facing `pluralRu(...)`. `2333` is subgroup guest count (`section.orders.length`), not a top-level section total. The prompt needs to define whether “guest count” means unique `order.guest`, unique guest per table/session, or fallback one guest per order when `guest` is missing.
- `Fix 2: Rewrite needed.` The cited structures are real: `activeOrders` at `3539-3544`, `filteredGroups` at `3792-3801`, `tabCounts` at `3804-3818`. But `orderGroups` does not carry session-open state, so “keep served table visible until manual close” is under-specified. `closeSession()` is shared in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` and is used by both StaffOrdersMobile and `partnertables`, so changing it would be cross-page scope.
- `Fix 3: Clear.` `2249-2252` and `2259-2262` are passive star-badge `div`s inside the clickable card at `2244`, and they do not stop propagation. The neighboring lock badge at `2255-2257` already does, so the intended change is straightforward.
- `Fix 4: Rewrite needed.` The four listed wrapper regions are real, but the prompt misses another live `inProgressExpanded` wrapper at `2346`. The shared state/effect at `1780`, `1816-1823` still assumes that wrapper exists, so editing only four branches will leave inconsistent behavior.

+### Fix 1 - Guest Counting via `.length` + `pluralRu`
+
+Rating: **Needs clarification**
+
+- The cited lines are real in the `260413` / `staffordersmobile.jsx` snapshot.
